1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

# Kafka ACL Authorization Code Audit

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in `apache/kafka` that implement or define Access Control List (ACL) authorization logic. Search under `core/src/main/` and `clients/src/main/` for files containing classes or interfaces with `Authorizer` or `AclAuthorizer` in the name. For each file, report the class name and whether it defines the interface, implements it, or provides test utilities.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

I've completed the audit of the Kafka codebase for ACL authorization logic. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I identified **17 Java source files** implementing ACL authorization in the Kafka codebase, organized into three main packages:

### Core Interfaces (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/)
- **Authorizer** - The main pluggable interface that all authorizer implementations must extend
- **AuthorizerServerInfo** - Runtime server metadata interface
- **AuthorizableRequestContext** - Request context interface
- **Action** - Authorization action class
- **AuthorizationResult** - Enum for authorization decisions
- **AclCreateResult, AclDeleteResult** - Result classes for ACL operations

### Implementation (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/)
- **ClusterMetadataAuthorizer** - Interface extending Authorizer for cluster-aware ACL operations
- **StandardAuthorizer** - The built-in production authorizer implementation storing ACLs in the metadata log
- **StandardAuthorizerData** - Core data container for ACL state
- **AclCache, AclMutator** - Support interfaces and classes
- **StandardAcl, StandardAclWithId, StandardAclRecordIterator** - Data classes for ACL management

### Utilities (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/)
- **AclEntry** - Data class representing individual ACL entries
- **AuthorizerUtils** - Factory utility for creating authorizer instances

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed information on each file, including file paths, class names, and a comprehensive explanation of how these components work together in the authorization framework.
